### [51] [Reasoning Models Sometimes Output Illegible Chains of Thought](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27338)
*Arun Jose*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Outcome-based RL often yields opaque CoTs—models hide reasoning in illegible tokens while keeping correct outputs, challenging monitoring without explicit legibility optimization.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understand whether CoTs from outcome-trained RL models are legible and faithful for monitoring intentions and detecting malicious behavior.

Method: Empirical evaluation across 14 reasoning models comparing legibility to humans and AI monitors, ablation forcing use of legible portions, resampling analyses, difficulty stratification, and hypothesis exploration.

Result: RL-trained models (except Claude) generate illegible CoTs yet maintain correct final answers; accuracy drops 53% when forced to use only legible portions; legibility declines on harder questions; no simple correlation between legibility and performance when resampling.

Conclusion: Outcome-based RL often makes chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning illegible while final answers remain readable, undermining monitoring efforts.

Abstract: Language models trained via outcome-based reinforcement learning (RL) to
reason using chain-of-thought (CoT) have shown remarkable performance.
Monitoring such a model's CoT may allow us to understand its intentions and
detect potential malicious behavior. However, to be effective, this requires
that CoTs are legible and faithful. We study CoT legibility across 14 reasoning
models, finding that RL often causes reasoning to become illegible to both
humans and AI monitors, with reasoning models (except Claude) generating
illegible CoTs while returning to perfectly readable final answers. We show
that models use illegible reasoning to reach correct answers (accuracy dropping
by 53\% when forced to use only legible portions), yet find no correlation
between legibility and performance when resampling - suggesting the
relationship is more nuanced. We also find that legibility degrades on harder
questions. We discuss potential hypotheses for these results, including
steganography, training artifacts, and vestigial tokens. These results suggest
that without explicit optimization for legibility, outcome-based RL naturally
produces models with increasingly opaque reasoning processes, potentially
undermining monitoring approaches.

</details>


### [52] [Measuring Chain-of-Thought Monitorability Through Faithfulness and Verbosity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27378)
*Austin Meek,Eitan Sprejer,Iván Arcuschin,Austin J. Brockmeier,Steven Basart*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 把faithfulness与新引入的verbosity结合为monitorability评分，用以衡量CoT作为外部工作记忆的可监控性，实验表明即便表面忠实也可能遗漏关键推理，且不同模型族表现差异大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有通过在输入加入提示并观察模型答案变化来检测CoT不忠实性的方法有局限，无法检测在答案不变时的遗漏或与提示无关的推理缺失。需要更全面衡量CoT对内部推理可监控性的能力，尤其是对安全相关监控的重要性。

Method: 引入verbosity概念并结合faithfulness构造monitorability分数；在BBH、GPQA、MMLU数据集上对指令微调与推理模型进行评估；使用Inspect库开源评测代码，以便复现。

Result: 实验结果表明：模型可能在常规不忠实性检测下显得忠实，但仍因遗漏关键因素而难以被监控；不同模型族在monitorability上差异显著；并开源了评测工具。

Conclusion: 论文认为链式思维（CoT）输出可以作为观察模型内部推理的窗口，但仅在CoT真实反映内部推理（faithfulness）且完整列出解决任务所需因素（verbosity）时才能用于安全监控（monitorability）。作者提出将faithfulness与verbosity合并为单一的monitorability评分，表征CoT作为模型“外部工作记忆”的能力，并在若干基准上评估模型显示不同模型族的monitorability差异。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) outputs let us read a model's step-by-step reasoning.
Since any long, serial reasoning process must pass through this textual trace,
the quality of the CoT is a direct window into what the model is thinking. This
visibility could help us spot unsafe or misaligned behavior (monitorability),
but only if the CoT is transparent about its internal reasoning (faithfulness).
Fully measuring faithfulness is difficult, so researchers often focus on
examining the CoT in cases where the model changes its answer after adding a
cue to the input. This proxy finds some instances of unfaithfulness but loses
information when the model maintains its answer, and does not investigate
aspects of reasoning not tied to the cue. We extend these results to a more
holistic sense of monitorability by introducing verbosity: whether the CoT
lists every factor needed to solve the task. We combine faithfulness and
verbosity into a single monitorability score that shows how well the CoT serves
as the model's external `working memory', a property that many safety schemes
based on CoT monitoring depend on. We evaluate instruction-tuned and reasoning
models on BBH, GPQA, and MMLU. Our results show that models can appear faithful
yet remain hard to monitor when they leave out key factors, and that
monitorability differs sharply across model families. We release our evaluation
code using the Inspect library to support reproducible future work.

</details>


### [53] [FedMuon: Accelerating Federated Learning with Matrix Orthogonalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27403)
*Junkang Liu,Fanhua Shang,Junchao Zhou,Hongying Liu,Yuanyuan Liu,Jin Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出针对矩阵参数的Muon优化器及联邦版本FedMuon，通过矩阵正交化、动量聚合与局部-全局对齐解决非IID下的客户端漂移问题，实现通信效率与收敛速度显著提升，并给出理论证明与实证结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦学习多使用逐元素优化器（如Adam/SGD），忽视了权重矩阵的几何结构，导致局部更新中病态方向放大、条件数恶化与收敛缓慢；需要更有效的本地更新以减少通信轮次。

Method: 在本地引入矩阵正交化的Muon优化器以保留权重的几何结构；针对非IID问题，提出FedMuon，包括（1）动量聚合：将服务端聚合后的动量下发作为客户端初始化，避免动量重置；（2）局部-全局对齐：对本地梯度与全局更新方向对齐以降低客户端漂移。理论上给出关于参与客户端数S、本地迭代次数K和通信轮次R的线性加速收敛率证明，同时在语言与视觉任务上做了实证验证。

Result: 在IID设置下，Local Muon显著加速收敛并减少通信轮次，优于Local SGD和Local AdamW；在非IID设置，通过FedMuon的两项技术成功抑制客户端漂移，降低通信轮次并提升测试精度；理论证明在无异质性假设下实现线性加速收敛。

Conclusion: 提出了在联邦学习环境中针对矩阵结构参数的本地优化器Muon及其联邦版本FedMuon，解决了局部矩阵正交化在非IID场景下导致的客户端漂移问题，并证明了FedMuon在不依赖同质性假设下仍可取得线性加速收敛。

Abstract: The core bottleneck of Federated Learning (FL) lies in the communication
rounds. That is, how to achieve more effective local updates is crucial for
reducing communication rounds. Existing FL methods still primarily use
element-wise local optimizers (Adam/SGD), neglecting the geometric structure of
the weight matrices. This often leads to the amplification of pathological
directions in the weights during local updates, leading deterioration in the
condition number and slow convergence. Therefore, we introduce the Muon
optimizer in local, which has matrix orthogonalization to optimize
matrix-structured parameters. Experimental results show that, in IID setting,
Local Muon significantly accelerates the convergence of FL and reduces
communication rounds compared to Local SGD and Local AdamW. However, in non-IID
setting, independent matrix orthogonalization based on the local distributions
of each client induces strong client drift. Applying Muon in non-IID FL poses
significant challenges: (1) client preconditioner leading to client drift; (2)
moment reinitialization. To address these challenges, we propose a novel
Federated Muon optimizer (FedMuon), which incorporates two key techniques: (1)
momentum aggregation, where clients use the aggregated momentum for local
initialization; (2) local-global alignment, where the local gradients are
aligned with the global update direction to significantly reduce client drift.
Theoretically, we prove that \texttt{FedMuon} achieves a linear speedup
convergence rate without the heterogeneity assumption, where $S$ is the number
of participating clients per round, $K$ is the number of local iterations, and
$R$ is the total number of communication rounds. Empirically, we validate the
effectiveness of FedMuon on language and vision models. Compared to several
baselines, FedMuon significantly reduces communication rounds and improves test
accuracy.

</details>


### [54] [Atlas-Alignment: Making Interpretability Transferable Across Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27413)
*Bruno Puri,Jim Berend,Sebastian Lapuschkin,Wojciech Samek*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 通过将新模型的潜在空间对齐到一个已标注的概念图谱，Atlas-Alignment 能以极低的边际成本实现语义检索与可控生成，免去为每个模型训练与标注专属解释器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可解释性流程昂贵且难以扩展：每个新模型需要训练模型专属的稀疏自编码器并进行手工或半自动标注。作者希望通过一次构建高质量的 Concept Atlas 来降低后续模型解释的边际成本。

Method: 使用共享输入与轻量级的表征对齐技术（例如线性映射或简单投影等）将目标模型的潜在表示对齐到 Concept Atlas；对齐后可进行语义特征搜索/检索与基于图谱概念的生成调控。

Result: 定量与定性评估表明，简单的表征对齐方法能够在无需标注概念数据的情况下，实现稳健的语义检索与可控生成，从而显著摊薄可解释性与机制可解释研究的成本。

Conclusion: Atlas-Alignment 提出了一种通过将未知模型的潜在空间对齐到一个已标注的人类可解释“概念图谱”（Concept Atlas）来实现可解释性迁移的框架，从而避免对每个新模型都训练专门的稀疏自编码器和标注组件。

Abstract: Interpretability is crucial for building safe, reliable, and controllable
language models, yet existing interpretability pipelines remain costly and
difficult to scale. Interpreting a new model typically requires costly training
of model-specific sparse autoencoders, manual or semi-automated labeling of SAE
components, and their subsequent validation. We introduce Atlas-Alignment, a
framework for transferring interpretability across language models by aligning
unknown latent spaces to a Concept Atlas - a labeled, human-interpretable
latent space - using only shared inputs and lightweight representational
alignment techniques. Once aligned, this enables two key capabilities in
previously opaque models: (1) semantic feature search and retrieval, and (2)
steering generation along human-interpretable atlas concepts. Through
quantitative and qualitative evaluations, we show that simple representational
alignment methods enable robust semantic retrieval and steerable generation
without the need for labeled concept data. Atlas-Alignment thus amortizes the
cost of explainable AI and mechanistic interpretability: by investing in one
high-quality Concept Atlas, we can make many new models transparent and
controllable at minimal marginal cost.

### [56] [Spectral Neural Graph Sparsification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27474)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图神经网络依赖固定结构并易受过度平滑影响，限制了它们在大规模图和需降维或稀疏化场景中的应用。作者希望通过生成保持谱信息的缩减图，既降低计算成本又保持下游任务性能。

Method: 核心方法包括Joint Graph Evolution层（联合演化层）和Spectral Concordance损失。联合演化层同时对图拓扑和节点特征进行逐层变换，使结构与属性共同演化，摆脱静态邻域聚合的局限；谱一致性损失通过约束图的谱属性和节点特征的一致性，正则化这些变换以确保缩减图作为原图的忠实代理。

Abstract: Graphs are central to modeling complex systems in domains such as social
networks, molecular chemistry, and neuroscience. While Graph Neural Networks,
particularly Graph Convolutional Networks, have become standard tools for graph
learning, they remain constrained by reliance on fixed structures and
susceptibility to over-smoothing. We propose the Spectral Preservation Network,
a new framework for graph representation learning that generates reduced graphs
serving as faithful proxies of the original, enabling downstream tasks such as
community detection, influence propagation, and information diffusion at a
reduced computational cost. The Spectral Preservation Network introduces two
key components: the Joint Graph Evolution layer and the Spectral Concordance
loss. The former jointly transforms both the graph topology and the node
feature matrix, allowing the structure and attributes to evolve adaptively
across layers and overcoming the rigidity of static neighborhood aggregation.
The latter regularizes these transformations by enforcing consistency in both
the spectral properties of the graph and the feature vectors of the nodes. We
evaluate the effectiveness of Spectral Preservation Network on node-level
sparsification by analyzing well-established metrics and benchmarking against
state-of-the-art methods. The experimental results demonstrate the superior
performance and clear advantages of our approach.

### [57] [Simplex-to-Euclidean Bijections for Categorical Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27480)
*Bernardo Williams,Victor M. Yeom-Song,Marcelo Hartmann,Arto Klami*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 通过Aitchison几何构造的光滑双射将单纯形映射到欧氏空间，并用Dirichlet插值去量化离散数据，从而在欧氏空间中进行有效密度建模并能精确恢复原始离散分布；方法相比直接在单纯形上工作的技术更易与欧氏建模工具结合，效果具有竞争力。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Aitchison几何构造光滑双射，将单纯形映射到欧氏空间，在欧氏空间中进行密度建模；为处理类别数据，采用Dirichlet插值对离散观测进行去量化（dequantize），从而既能在欧氏空间建模又能精确恢复原始离散分布。

Result: 在合成数据与真实数据集上，该方法与现有在单纯形上工作的先进方法相比表现具有竞争力，既保留了几何结构又能实现精确的离散分布恢复。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了在单纯形上进行概率分布学习与采样的可行方法，通过将开单纯形与欧氏空间建立光滑双射映射来实现。

Abstract: We propose a method for learning and sampling from probability distributions
supported on the simplex. Our approach maps the open simplex to Euclidean space
via smooth bijections, leveraging the Aitchison geometry to define the
mappings, and supports modeling categorical data by a Dirichlet interpolation
that dequantizes discrete observations into continuous ones. This enables
density modeling in Euclidean space through the bijection while still allowing
exact recovery of the original discrete distribution. Compared to previous
methods that operate on the simplex using Riemannian geometry or custom noise
processes, our approach works in Euclidean space while respecting the Aitchison
geometry, and achieves competitive performance on both synthetic and real-world
data sets.

### [58] [Thought Branches: Interpreting LLM Reasoning Requires Resampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27484)
*Uzay Macar,Paul C. Bogdan,Senthooran Rajamanoharan,Neel Nanda*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 仅看单一路径不足以理解CoT因果性。通过重采样研究CoT分布可更可靠地评估哪些句子实际影响决策、哪种干预有效，以及隐含提示的累积作用，且提出恢复性指标与基于重采样的在策略干预作为改进手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大多数解释推理模型的工作仅研究单一CoT样本，但模型实际上对众多可能CoT定义了分布；单样本研究不足以理解因果影响与底层计算，因此需要通过采样探索分布以获得更可靠的因果推断与干预手段。

Method: 提出对CoT进行重采样的实证方法：在不同场景中通过替换或重复采样句子／完成来测量其对下游决策的因果影响，并引入‘恢复性’指标以评估移除推理步骤的持久性，同时借鉴因果中介分析研究隐藏提示的累积影响。

Result: 通过多项案例研究发现：自我保全类句子对诱导黑mail的影响很小，表明并非主要驱动因素；离策略（off-policy）的人工编辑对引导决策影响小且不稳定，而重采样可稳定且有效地选出所需特性；关键规划语句难以移除且其删除对行为影响大；隐含提示虽未显式出现但通过微妙累积影响CoT并对输出产生因果作用。总体上，重采样使因果分析更可靠，便于解释模型推理并进行有原则的CoT干预。

Conclusion: 研究表明，仅考察单一连贯推理路径（CoT）无法充分揭示大型语言模型的因果机制，需要通过重采样分析CoT分布以得到可靠结论。

Abstract: Most work interpreting reasoning models studies only a single
chain-of-thought (CoT), yet these models define distributions over many
possible CoTs. We argue that studying a single sample is inadequate for
understanding causal influence and the underlying computation. Though fully
specifying this distribution is intractable, it can be understood by sampling.
We present case studies using resampling to investigate model decisions. First,
when a model states a reason for its action, does that reason actually cause
the action? In "agentic misalignment" scenarios, we resample specific sentences
to measure their downstream effects. Self-preservation sentences have small
causal impact, suggesting they do not meaningfully drive blackmail. Second, are
artificial edits to CoT sufficient for steering reasoning? These are common in
literature, yet take the model off-policy. Resampling and selecting a
completion with the desired property is a principled on-policy alternative. We
find off-policy interventions yield small and unstable effects compared to
resampling in decision-making tasks. Third, how do we understand the effect of
removing a reasoning step when the model may repeat it post-edit? We introduce
a resilience metric that repeatedly resamples to prevent similar content from
reappearing downstream. Critical planning statements resist removal but have
large effects when eliminated. Fourth, since CoT is sometimes "unfaithful", can
our methods teach us anything in these settings? Adapting causal mediation
analysis, we find that hints that have a causal effect on the output without
being explicitly mentioned exert a subtle and cumulative influence on the CoT
that persists even if the hint is removed. Overall, studying distributions via
resampling enables reliable causal analysis, clearer narratives of model
reasoning, and principled CoT interventions.

### [59] [FedAdamW: A Communication-Efficient Optimizer with Convergence and Generalization Guarantees for Federated Large Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27486)
*Junkang Liu,Fanhua Shang,Kewen Zhu,Hongying Liu,Yuanyuan Liu,Jin Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FedAdamW：为联邦学习定制的AdamW，通过本地校正、解耦权重衰减与二阶矩均值聚合来降低方差、抑制过拟合并加速收敛，理论与实验证明其优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接将AdamW用于联邦学习会遇到三个主要问题：数据异质性使二阶矩估计方差大，本地AdamW导致局部过拟合与客户端漂移，以及每轮重置动量估计会减慢收敛，因此需要设计适配联邦场景的AdamW算法。

Method: 提出FedAdamW：1) 本地校正机制使局部更新与全局更新一致；2) 采用解耦权重衰减在本地训练中抑制过拟合；3) 聚合各客户端二阶动量估计的均值以降低方差并重新初始化动量；4) 理论证明收敛性并用PAC-贝叶斯给出泛化分析；5) 在语言与视觉Transformer上进行广泛对比实验。

Result: 理论上在没有异质性假设下给出线性加速的收敛率：O( sqrt((L Δ σ_l^2)/(S K R ε^2)) + (L Δ)/R )，并通过PAC-贝叶斯分析解释了解耦权重衰减的效果。实验结果表明FedAdamW在语言和视觉Transformer上较基线显著减少通信轮次并提高测试准确率。

Conclusion: 论文提出了FedAdamW，一种在联邦学习中使用AdamW的算法，通过局部校正、解耦权重衰减和对二阶矩估计的均值聚合及重初始化，解决了数据异质性导致的二阶矩方差高、局部过拟合和动量重置慢收敛等问题。理论上在无异质性假设下证明了线性加速的收敛率，并用PAC-贝叶斯分析说明了解耦权重衰减的泛化优势；实验证明在Transformer上通信轮次减少且测试准确率提升。

Abstract: AdamW has become one of the most effective optimizers for training
large-scale models. We have also observed its effectiveness in the context of
federated learning (FL). However, directly applying AdamW in federated learning
settings poses significant challenges: (1) due to data heterogeneity, AdamW
often yields high variance in the second-moment estimate $\boldsymbol{v}$; (2)
the local overfitting of AdamW may cause client drift; and (3) Reinitializing
moment estimates ($\boldsymbol{v}$, $\boldsymbol{m}$) at each round slows down
convergence. To address these challenges, we propose the first
\underline{Fed}erated \underline{AdamW} algorithm, called \texttt{FedAdamW},
for training and fine-tuning various large models. \texttt{FedAdamW} aligns
local updates with the global update using both a \textbf{local correction
mechanism} and decoupled weight decay to mitigate local overfitting.
\texttt{FedAdamW} efficiently aggregates the \texttt{mean} of the second-moment
estimates to reduce their variance and reinitialize them. Theoretically, we
prove that \texttt{FedAdamW} achieves a linear speedup convergence rate of
$\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{(L \Delta \sigma_l^2)/(S K R \epsilon^2)}+(L \Delta)/R)$
without \textbf{heterogeneity assumption}, where $S$ is the number of
participating clients per round, $K$ is the number of local iterations, and $R$
is the total number of communication rounds. We also employ PAC-Bayesian
generalization analysis to explain the effectiveness of decoupled weight decay
in local training. Empirically, we validate the effectiveness of
\texttt{FedAdamW} on language and vision Transformer models. Compared to
several baselines, \texttt{FedAdamW} significantly reduces communication rounds
and improves test accuracy. The code is available in
https://github.com/junkangLiu0/FedAdamW.

</details>


### [60] [InertialAR: Autoregressive 3D Molecule Generation with Inertial Frames](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27497)
*Haorui Li,Weitao Du,Yuqiang Li,Hongyu Guo,Shengchao Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: InertialAR aligns molecules to inertial frames for invariant tokenization, adds GeoRoPE for geometric attention, and uses hierarchical autoregressive + diffusion for coordinate generation, achieving strong empirical results.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Extend transformer-based autoregressive models to 3D molecule generation by solving tokenization and architecture challenges for SE(3)/permutation invariance and hybrid discrete-continuous tokens.

Method: Canonical tokenization via inertial frame alignment and atom reordering for SE(3) and permutation invariance; geometric rotary positional encoding (GeoRoPE) for attention; hierarchical autoregressive prediction predicting atom type then coordinates with a diffusion loss.

Result: State-of-the-art on 7/10 unconditional generation metrics across QM9, GEOM-Drugs, B3LYP; SOTA on all 5 controllable generation metrics.

Conclusion: Paper proposes InertialAR for 3D molecule generation, achieving SOTA on multiple metrics and excelling in controllable generation.

Abstract: Transformer-based autoregressive models have emerged as a unifying paradigm
across modalities such as text and images, but their extension to 3D molecule
generation remains underexplored. The gap stems from two fundamental
challenges: (1) tokenizing molecules into a canonical 1D sequence of tokens
that is invariant to both SE(3) transformations and atom index permutations,
and (2) designing an architecture capable of modeling hybrid atom-based tokens
that couple discrete atom types with continuous 3D coordinates. To address
these challenges, we introduce InertialAR. InertialAR devises a canonical
tokenization that aligns molecules to their inertial frames and reorders atoms
to ensure SE(3) and permutation invariance. Moreover, InertialAR equips the
attention mechanism with geometric awareness via geometric rotary positional
encoding (GeoRoPE). In addition, it utilizes a hierarchical autoregressive
paradigm to predict the next atom-based token, predicting the atom type first
and then its 3D coordinates via Diffusion loss. Experimentally, InertialAR
achieves state-of-the-art performance on 7 of the 10 evaluation metrics for
unconditional molecule generation across QM9, GEOM-Drugs, and B3LYP. Moreover,
it significantly outperforms strong baselines in controllable generation for
targeted chemical functionality, attaining state-of-the-art results across all
5 metrics.

### [61] [DP-FedPGN: Finding Global Flat Minima for Differentially Private Federated Learning via Penalizing Gradient Norm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27504)
*Junkang Liu,Yuxuan Tian,Fanhua Shang,Yuanyuan Liu,Hongying Liu,Junchao Zhou,Daorui Ding*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DP-FedPGN在本地损失加入全局梯度范数惩罚，寻求全局平坦极小值以改善CL-DPFL下的泛化和收敛，同时保持严格的差分隐私。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有客户级差分隐私联邦学习方法造成损失曲面变陡，模型泛化能力下降；局部平坦性（如SAM）无法保证全局平坦性，需设计能够寻求全局平坦极小值的机制以改善性能和减小裁剪误差。

Method: 提出DP-FedPGN算法：在客户端本地目标中加入全局梯度范数惩罚项以寻求全局平坦极小值，同时配合梯度裁剪与R e9nyi DP机制给出严格隐私保证，并对局部更新灵敏度做分析。

Result: 理论证明DP-FedPGN减轻了差分隐私带来的性能退化，并能消除数据异质性影响且加快收敛；在ResNet和Transformer上的六个视觉与NLP任务上显著优于现有最先进算法；提供了R e9nyi DP级别的隐私保证和局部更新灵敏度分析。

Conclusion: DP-FedPGN通过在局部损失中引入全局梯度范数惩罚，能在保证差分隐私的同时找到更平的全局极小值，减轻DP导致的泛化性能下降，并消除数据异质性影响，收敛更快。

Abstract: To prevent inference attacks in Federated Learning (FL) and reduce the
leakage of sensitive information, Client-level Differentially Private Federated
Learning (CL-DPFL) is widely used. However, current CL-DPFL methods usually
result in sharper loss landscapes, which leads to a decrease in model
generalization after differential privacy protection. By using Sharpness Aware
Minimization (SAM), the current popular federated learning methods are to find
a local flat minimum value to alleviate this problem. However, the local
flatness may not reflect the global flatness in CL-DPFL. Therefore, to address
this issue and seek global flat minima of models, we propose a new CL-DPFL
algorithm, DP-FedPGN, in which we introduce a global gradient norm penalty to
the local loss to find the global flat minimum. Moreover, by using our global
gradient norm penalty, we not only find a flatter global minimum but also
reduce the locally updated norm, which means that we further reduce the error
of gradient clipping. From a theoretical perspective, we analyze how DP-FedPGN
mitigates the performance degradation caused by DP. Meanwhile, the proposed
DP-FedPGN algorithm eliminates the impact of data heterogeneity and achieves
fast convergence. We also use R\'enyi DP to provide strict privacy guarantees
and provide sensitivity analysis for local updates. Finally, we conduct
effectiveness tests on both ResNet and Transformer models, and achieve
significant improvements in six visual and natural language processing tasks
compared to existing state-of-the-art algorithms. The code is available at
https://github.com/junkangLiu0/DP-FedPGN

</details>

Method: 比较两种预训练范式：在异构真实世界时间序列上预训练与在纯合成数据上预训练，再将模型微调用于两项EEG下游任务（运动意象分类与睡眠分期），并与EEGNet和CBraMod基线比较性能。

Conclusion: 该论文展示了通用时间序列基础模型可有效迁移到脑电（EEG）领域，即便预训练数据来自非神经源或合成信号。

Abstract: Foundation models for time series are emerging as powerful general-purpose
backbones, yet their potential for domain-specific biomedical signals such as
electroencephalography (EEG) remains rather unexplored. In this work, we
investigate the applicability a recently proposed time series classification
foundation model, to a different EEG tasks such as motor imagery classification
and sleep stage prediction. We test two pretraining regimes: (a) pretraining on
heterogeneous real-world time series from multiple domains, and (b) pretraining
on purely synthetic data. We find that both variants yield strong performance,
consistently outperforming EEGNet, a widely used convolutional baseline, and
CBraMod, the most recent EEG-specific foundation model. These results suggest
that generalist time series foundation models, even when pretrained on data of
non-neural origin or on synthetic signals, can transfer effectively to EEG. Our
findings highlight the promise of leveraging cross-domain pretrained models for
brain signal analysis, suggesting that EEG may benefit from advances in the
broader time series literature.

### [63] [Learning Sparse Approximate Inverse Preconditioners for Conjugate Gradient Solvers on GPUs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27517)
*Zherui Yang,Zhehao Li,Kangbo Lyu,Yixuan Li,Tao Du,Ligang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 使用GNN生成稀疏近似逆预条件子并设计尺度不变损失，可在GPU上显著加速CG求解并提升条件数与泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统预条件子（如不完全分解）在GPU上受限于三角求解的串行性和GNN难以建模的长程依赖；需要一种既能利用数据优化又能高效并行的预条件子生成方式。

Method: 用GNN直接生成GPU友好的SPAI预条件子，利用局部性的矩阵向量乘与GNN的传播机制匹配；提出基于统计的尺度不变损失函数，以考虑CG收敛率依赖条件数而非矩阵绝对尺度的特性。

Result: 在三个人工PDE数据集和一个合成数据集上，所提方法在GPU上比标准预条件子（对角、IC、传统SPAI）和先前学习方法更快，解算时间减少40%-53%（即68%-113%更快），并改善条件数与泛化。

Conclusion: 该论文提出一种基于GNN的学习方法用于构建稀疏近似逆（SPAI）预条件子，以提高共轭梯度（CG）在GPU上的求解效率，避免三角求解造成的串行瓶颈，取得了明显的加速与更好的条件数和泛化性能。

Abstract: The conjugate gradient solver (CG) is a prevalent method for solving
symmetric and positive definite linear systems Ax=b, where effective
preconditioners are crucial for fast convergence. Traditional preconditioners
rely on prescribed algorithms to offer rigorous theoretical guarantees, while
limiting their ability to exploit optimization from data. Existing
learning-based methods often utilize Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) to improve
the performance and speed up the construction. However, their reliance on
incomplete factorization leads to significant challenges: the associated
triangular solve hinders GPU parallelization in practice, and introduces
long-range dependencies which are difficult for GNNs to model. To address these
issues, we propose a learning-based method to generate GPU-friendly
preconditioners, particularly using GNNs to construct Sparse Approximate
Inverse (SPAI) preconditioners, which avoids triangular solves and requires
only two matrix-vector products at each CG step. The locality of matrix-vector
product is compatible with the local propagation mechanism of GNNs. The
flexibility of GNNs also allows our approach to be applied in a wide range of
scenarios. Furthermore, we introduce a statistics-based scale-invariant loss
function. Its design matches CG's property that the convergence rate depends on
the condition number, rather than the absolute scale of A, leading to improved
performance of the learned preconditioner. Evaluations on three PDE-derived
datasets and one synthetic dataset demonstrate that our method outperforms
standard preconditioners (Diagonal, IC, and traditional SPAI) and previous
learning-based preconditioners on GPUs. We reduce solution time on GPUs by
40%-53% (68%-113% faster), along with better condition numbers and superior
generalization performance. Source code available at
https://github.com/Adversarr/LearningSparsePreconditioner4GPU

*Yuxiang Chen,Xiaoming Xu,Pengle Zhang,Michael Beyer,Martin Rapp,Jun Zhu,Jianfei Chen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 降低大模型训练成本，使4-bit完全量化训练在效率提升同时保持接近全精度的训练性能。

Method: 采用NVFP4格式对所有线性层的激活、权重与梯度进行量化；提出无偏双块量化（double-block quantization）以减少量化误差；引入OsciReset抑制权重振荡；引入OutControl处理异常值。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) training is prohibitively expensive, driving

formats like NVFP4 offer substantial efficiency gains, achieving near-lossless

performance gap to full-precision training by an average of 51.3%.

transfer learning -- in the form of domain adaptation (DA) -- can be used to

effectiveness of this methodology is evaluated on a population of experimental
bridges. Specifically, this population includes data corresponding to several
damage states, as well as, a comprehensive set of environmental conditions. It
is found that combining transfer learning and active learning can improve data
efficiency when learning classification models in label-scarce scenarios. This
result has implications for data-informed operation and maintenance of
structures, suggesting a reduction in inspections over the operational lifetime

### [66] [Information-Theoretic Greedy Layer-wise Training for Traffic Sign Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27651)
*Shuyan Lyu,Zhanzimo Wu,Junliang Du*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文基于对CNN训练动态的信息论分析，提出一种结合确定性信息瓶颈与矩阵基R\'enyi熵的逐层贪婪训练方法：每层与辅助分类器联合训练以学习最小充分表示，减少内存和反向传播需求，在CIFAR和交通标志任务上优于已有分层方法并接近端到端SGD性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 端到端交叉熵+反向传播在生物可解释性、内存占用（需存储中间激活）、以及梯度消失/爆炸问题等方面存在局限；贪婪的分层训练能消除反向传播和交叉熵依赖、降低内存并缓解梯度问题，但现有方法多在小数据与简单架构上测试，缺乏对现代深度CNN的系统性分析与有效方法。

Method: 对流行卷积神经网络的训练动态进行信息论分析，使用矩阵基R\'enyi熵估计器测量层间信息，基于确定性信息瓶颈（DIB）构建目标函数，逐层训练：每层与直接连到输出层的辅助分类器联合训练以鼓励最小充分表示，从而避免反向传播和存储中间激活；在CIFAR-10/CIFAR-100及交通标志数据集上做实验比较。

Result: 通过信息论分析发现网络训练表现出自底向上的逐层收敛及马尔可夫信息瓶颈结构；提出的DIB+矩阵基R\'enyi方法在多个数据集和现代CNN上优于其他分层训练基线，且在准确率上接近或达到端到端SGD训练。

Conclusion: 本文提出一种基于确定性信息瓶颈（DIB）和矩阵基R\'enyi\'s α阶熵泛函的分层训练方法，通过对卷积神经网络(SGD训练)的训练动态进行信息论分析，发现网络按层自底向上收敛且信息流遵循马尔可夫信息瓶颈原则，从而设计每层与辅助分类器联合训练以学习最小充分的任务相关表征；在CIFAR-10、CIFAR-100及交通标志识别任务上，方法优于现有分层训练基线并可与端到端SGD性能相当。

Abstract: Modern deep neural networks (DNNs) are typically trained with a global
cross-entropy loss in a supervised end-to-end manner: neurons need to store
their outgoing weights; training alternates between a forward pass
(computation) and a top-down backward pass (learning) which is biologically
implausible. Alternatively, greedy layer-wise training eliminates the need for
cross-entropy loss and backpropagation. By avoiding the computation of
intermediate gradients and the storage of intermediate outputs, it reduces
memory usage and helps mitigate issues such as vanishing or exploding
gradients. However, most existing layer-wise training approaches have been
evaluated only on relatively small datasets with simple deep architectures. In
this paper, we first systematically analyze the training dynamics of popular
convolutional neural networks (CNNs) trained by stochastic gradient descent
(SGD) through an information-theoretic lens. Our findings reveal that networks
converge layer-by-layer from bottom to top and that the flow of information
adheres to a Markov information bottleneck principle. Building on these
observations, we propose a novel layer-wise training approach based on the
recently developed deterministic information bottleneck (DIB) and the
matrix-based R\'enyi's $\alpha$-order entropy functional. Specifically, each
layer is trained jointly with an auxiliary classifier that connects directly to
the output layer, enabling the learning of minimal sufficient task-relevant
representations. We empirically validate the effectiveness of our training
procedure on CIFAR-10 and CIFAR-100 using modern deep CNNs and further
demonstrate its applicability to a practical task involving traffic sign
recognition. Our approach not only outperforms existing layer-wise training
baselines but also achieves performance comparable to SGD.

</details>

### [68] [Challenges in Credit Assignment for Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning in Open Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27659)

  <summary>Details</summary>

system. Specifically, there are three types of openness as reported in (Eck et
al. 2023) [2]: agent openness, where agents can enter or leave the system at
any time; task openness, where new tasks emerge, and existing ones evolve or
disappear; and type openness, where the capabil-ities and behaviors of agents
change over time. This report provides a conceptual and empirical review,
focusing on the interplay between openness and the credit assignment problem
(CAP). CAP involves determining the contribution of individual agents to the

### [69] [ORGEval: Graph-Theoretic Evaluation of LLMs in Optimization Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27610)
*Zhuohan Wang,Ziwei Zhu,Ziniu Li,Congliang Chen,Yizhou Han,Yufeng Lin,Zhihang Lin,Angyang Gu,Xinglin Hu,Ruoyu Sun,Tian Ding*

TL;DR: ORGEval maps optimization models to graphs and uses an SD-aware WL-test to reliably detect model equivalence, providing a fast, robust evaluation method and benchmarks showing LLMs struggle but some models perform relatively better.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing solver-based evaluation of LLM-generated optimization models is unreliable (inconsistency, infeasibility, high cost); need robust, scalable metric focusing on structural equivalence.

Method: Represent optimization models as graphs, detect equivalence via graph isomorphism using a tailored Weisfeiler-Lehman (WL) test combined with symmetric decomposable (SD) detection to ensure WL correctness; construct Bench4Opt dataset and benchmark LLMs.

Result: ORGEval achieves 100% consistency across random parameterizations, outperforms solver-based methods in runtime especially on hard problems, and benchmarking shows DeepSeek-V3 and Claude-Opus-4 lead in accuracy for direct prompting.

Conclusion: The paper introduces ORGEval, a graph-theoretic framework for evaluating LLMs in formulating linear and mixed-integer linear programs, proving conditions under which WL-test guarantees correct isomorphism detection, and demonstrating robust, efficient equivalence detection and benchmarking results showing varied LLM performance.

Abstract: Formulating optimization problems for industrial applications demands
significant manual effort and domain expertise. While Large Language Models
(LLMs) show promise in automating this process, evaluating their performance
remains difficult due to the absence of robust metrics. Existing solver-based
approaches often face inconsistency, infeasibility issues, and high
computational costs. To address these issues, we propose ORGEval, a
graph-theoretic evaluation framework for assessing LLMs' capabilities in
formulating linear and mixed-integer linear programs. ORGEval represents
optimization models as graphs, reducing equivalence detection to graph
isomorphism testing. We identify and prove a sufficient condition, when the
tested graphs are symmetric decomposable (SD), under which the
Weisfeiler-Lehman (WL) test is guaranteed to correctly detect isomorphism.
Building on this, ORGEval integrates a tailored variant of the WL-test with an
SD detection algorithm to evaluate model equivalence. By focusing on structural
equivalence rather than instance-level configurations, ORGEval is robust to
numerical variations. Experimental results show that our method can
successfully detect model equivalence and produce 100\% consistent results
across random parameter configurations, while significantly outperforming
solver-based methods in runtime, especially on difficult problems. Leveraging
ORGEval, we construct the Bench4Opt dataset and benchmark state-of-the-art LLMs
on optimization modeling. Our results reveal that although optimization
modeling remains challenging for all LLMs, DeepSeek-V3 and Claude-Opus-4
achieve the highest accuracies under direct prompting, outperforming even
leading reasoning models.

Method: 定义panprediction框架并将其上游关系于omniprediction和multi-group learning；设计确定性与随机性panpredictor学习算法，分别给出\~O(1/ε^3)和\~O(1/ε^2)的样本复杂度；通过构造到step calibration（一种近无损的校准概念）的归约实现关键技术步骤。

Result: 给出确定性与随机性panpredictor样本复杂度界，改进确定性omniprediction已有界1/ε因子，并匹配其他已知omniprediction与multi-group学习界；证明在温和假设下，泛任务大量损失同时最小化并不比单任务单损失更难。

Conclusion: 该论文提出并形式化了panprediction范式，证明在温和条件下可用与单任务单损失同阶样本复杂度同时最小化无限多任务与损失。

Abstract: Supervised learning is classically formulated as training a model to minimize
a fixed loss function over a fixed distribution, or task. However, an emerging
paradigm instead views model training as extracting enough information from
data so that the model can be used to minimize many losses on many downstream
tasks. We formalize a mathematical framework for this paradigm, which we call
panprediction, and study its statistical complexity. Formally, panprediction
generalizes omniprediction and sits upstream from multi-group learning, which
respectively focus on predictions that generalize to many downstream losses or
many downstream tasks, but not both. Concretely, we design algorithms that
learn deterministic and randomized panpredictors with
$\tilde{O}(1/\varepsilon^3)$ and $\tilde{O}(1/\varepsilon^2)$ samples,
respectively. Our results demonstrate that under mild assumptions,
simultaneously minimizing infinitely many losses on infinitely many tasks can
be as statistically easy as minimizing one loss on one task. Along the way, we
improve the best known sample complexity guarantee of deterministic
omniprediction by a factor of $1/\varepsilon$, and match all other known sample
complexity guarantees of omniprediction and multi-group learning. Our key
technical ingredient is a nearly lossless reduction from panprediction to a
statistically efficient notion of calibration, called step calibration.

</details>


### [71] [Imbalanced Classification through the Lens of Spurious Correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27650)
*Jakob Hackstein,Sidney Bender*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 把类别不均衡看作放大Clever Hans问题的数据条件，用反事实解释检测并消除模型对非因果特征的依赖，从而在保持性能的同时提高模型的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统处理类别不均衡的方法多集中于数据重采样或损失重加权，但忽视了不均衡会导致模型对少数类出现欠确定性，从而放大CH效应，即模型借助非本质特征做出判定。作者期望通过可解释性技术直接识别并去除这些CH依赖。

Method: 基于反事实解释，联合检测与干预CH效应：生成或利用反事实样本来揭示模型依赖的非因果特征（CH证据），并对这些证据进行去除或校正；同时在训练或后处理阶段调整决策以减弱对少数类的误导性特征依赖。

Result: 在三个数据集上，该方法取得了有竞争力的分类性能，并通过可视化或实例分析展示了在不均衡场景下CH效应的出现与被缓解的过程。

Conclusion: 本文将类别不均衡视为导致Clever Hans（CH）现象扩大的数据条件，通过反事实解释方法和可解释AI识别并消除在不均衡下出现的CH效应，从而改善分类器鲁棒性。

Abstract: Class imbalance poses a fundamental challenge in machine learning, frequently
leading to unreliable classification performance. While prior methods focus on
data- or loss-reweighting schemes, we view imbalance as a data condition that
amplifies Clever Hans (CH) effects by underspecification of minority classes.
In a counterfactual explanations-based approach, we propose to leverage
Explainable AI to jointly identify and eliminate CH effects emerging under
imbalance. Our method achieves competitive classification performance on three
datasets and demonstrates how CH effects emerge under imbalance, a perspective
largely overlooked by existing approaches.

</details>

### [72] [VISAT: Benchmarking Adversarial and Distribution Shift Robustness in Traffic Sign Recognition with Visual Attributes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26833)
*Simon Yu,Peilin Yu,Hongbo Zheng,Huajie Shao,Han Zhao,Lui Sha*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: VISAT是在MTSD基础上增加视觉属性标注，提供对抗攻击与分布偏移两个鲁棒性基准，发现对抗攻击、腐扰和属性间虚假相关性都会显著影响交通标志识别模型表现，比较了ResNet-152与ViT-B/32以及单任务/多任务模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在现实驾驶场景中，视觉属性如何影响交通标志识别模型的鲁棒性，尤其在面对对抗攻击与分布偏移时，评估多任务学习是否会引入或放大发现的虚假相关性。

Method: 在MTSD基础上构建VISAT，加入属性标注（颜色、形状、符号、文本）；构建两类基准：1) 使用PGD生成对抗样本评估基线与MTL模型；2) 使用ImageNet-C的腐扰和自然变体评估分布偏移鲁棒性，并通过颜色量化合成改变测试虚假相关性。比较ResNet-152和ViT-B/32的性能。

Result: 实验证明PGD对模型（尤其是基线模型）有显著破坏效果；MTL模型在某些属性任务上表现更好但也更易受属性间的虚假相关性影响；分布偏移（ImageNet-C腐扰与颜色量化）普遍降低了准确率；不同主干（ResNet-152 vs ViT-B/32）在鲁棒性上存在差异。

Conclusion: VISAT数据集和基准套件展示了在交通标志识别任务中评估模型对视觉属性影响下的鲁棒性的重要性；实验表明对抗攻击和分布偏移都会显著降低模型性能，并暴露了多任务学习模型中存在的虚假相关性。

Abstract: We present VISAT, a novel open dataset and benchmarking suite for evaluating
model robustness in the task of traffic sign recognition with the presence of
visual attributes. Built upon the Mapillary Traffic Sign Dataset (MTSD), our
dataset introduces two benchmarks that respectively emphasize robustness
against adversarial attacks and distribution shifts. For our adversarial attack
benchmark, we employ the state-of-the-art Projected Gradient Descent (PGD)
method to generate adversarial inputs and evaluate their impact on popular
models. Additionally, we investigate the effect of adversarial attacks on
attribute-specific multi-task learning (MTL) networks, revealing spurious
correlations among MTL tasks. The MTL networks leverage visual attributes
(color, shape, symbol, and text) that we have created for each traffic sign in
our dataset. For our distribution shift benchmark, we utilize ImageNet-C's
realistic data corruption and natural variation techniques to perform
evaluations on the robustness of both base and MTL models. Moreover, we further
explore spurious correlations among MTL tasks through synthetic alterations of
traffic sign colors using color quantization techniques. Our experiments focus
on two major backbones, ResNet-152 and ViT-B/32, and compare the performance
between base and MTL models. The VISAT dataset and benchmarking framework
contribute to the understanding of model robustness for traffic sign
recognition, shedding light on the challenges posed by adversarial attacks and
distribution shifts. We believe this work will facilitate advancements in
developing more robust models for real-world applications in autonomous driving
and cyber-physical systems.

</details>


### [73] [Broken-Token: Filtering Obfuscated Prompts by Counting Characters-Per-Token](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26847)
*Shaked Zychlinski,Yuval Kainan*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 利用BPE分词器对异常编码文本产生更短更多标记的特性，基于平均字符/标记比(CPT)设阈值即可低成本高效检测并阻止伪装的prompt jailbreak攻击。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有防护多依赖专门LLM或困惑度模型，计算成本高，且对使用密码学或字符级编码的绕过手段无效。寻找一种低成本、模型无关且能实时部署的检测方法。

Method: 通过统计输入文本的平均字符数/标记数(CPT)，并设定阈值来区分天然语言与异常编码文本，基于BPE分词器在遇到离群文本时会拆分为更多短标记的现象。实验在十万级提示数据集和多种编码方案、常见分词器上评估，比较不同阈值的检测性能。

Result: 在超过100,000条提示和多种编码/分词器组合上，简单的CPT阈值策略以近乎完美的准确率区分编码文本与自然语言，包含对短文本的鲁棒性；方法开销极小，适合实时过滤和离线数据清洗。

Conclusion: 提出基于字符/标记比(CPT)的轻量级检测方法，可以有效识别使用替换、转码等编码方式伪装的恶意提示，适用于多种BPE分词器，计算成本低，部署简便。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are susceptible to jailbreak attacks where
malicious prompts are disguised using ciphers and character-level encodings to
bypass safety guardrails. While these guardrails often fail to interpret the
encoded content, the underlying models can still process the harmful
instructions. We introduce CPT-Filtering, a novel, model-agnostic with
negligible-costs and near-perfect accuracy guardrail technique that aims to
mitigate these attacks by leveraging the intrinsic behavior of Byte-Pair
Encoding (BPE) tokenizers. Our method is based on the principle that
tokenizers, trained on natural language, represent out-of-distribution text,
such as ciphers, using a significantly higher number of shorter tokens. Our
technique uses a simple yet powerful artifact of using language models: the
average number of Characters Per Token (CPT) in the text. This approach is
motivated by the high compute cost of modern methods - relying on added modules
such as dedicated LLMs or perplexity models. We validate our approach across a
large dataset of over 100,000 prompts, testing numerous encoding schemes with
several popular tokenizers. Our experiments demonstrate that a simple CPT
threshold robustly identifies encoded text with high accuracy, even for very
short inputs. CPT-Filtering provides a practical defense layer that can be
immediately deployed for real-time text filtering and offline data curation.

</details>

Conclusion: 该论文提出了一个结合传统机器学习与大语言模型（LLM）的混合框架，用于物联网（IoT）攻击检测、行为分析与缓解建议，并在多个数据集和评估器上进行了定量评估，结果显示随机森林在检测任务上表现最好，ChatGPT-o3在分析与缓解建议上优于DeepSeek-R1。

Abstract: The Internet of Things has expanded rapidly, transforming communication and
operations across industries but also increasing the attack surface and
security breaches. Artificial Intelligence plays a key role in securing IoT,
enabling attack detection, attack behavior analysis, and mitigation suggestion.
Despite advancements, evaluations remain purely qualitative, and the lack of a
standardized, objective benchmark for quantitatively measuring AI-based attack
analysis and mitigation hinders consistent assessment of model effectiveness.
In this work, we propose a hybrid framework combining Machine Learning (ML) for
multi-class attack detection with Large Language Models (LLMs) for attack
behavior analysis and mitigation suggestion. After benchmarking several ML and

applied structured role-play prompt engineering with Retrieval-Augmented

responses. Results show that Random Forest has the best detection model, and

### [75] [Adapting Large Language Models to Emerging Cybersecurity using Retrieval Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27080)
*Arnabh Borah,Md Tanvirul Alam,Nidhi Rastogi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 本文提出了基于RAG的框架，用于将外部网络安全数据与LLM结合，以提高模型在知识保持和时间推理任务上的准确性和可解释性。实验表明，混合检索策略优于基线RAG，在多个评估指标上显著提升了对新兴漏洞和攻击模式的检测能力。

contextualize cybersecurity data and enhance LLM accuracy in knowledge

### [76] [Lightweight CNN Model Hashing with Higher-Order Statistics and Chaotic Mapping for Piracy Detection and Tamper Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27127)
*Kunming Yang,Ling Chen*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出无需训练的轻量级CNN模型哈希：用偏度、峰度与结构特征+混沌映射构建鲁棒且判别的感知哈希，能高效检测盗版并定位篡改。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于感知哈希的方法要么依赖额外神经网络训练，资源消耗大，要么适用性差不能普适于所有CNN，因而需要一种轻量、无需训练且适用范围广的模型哈希方法。

Method: 直接从每层网络参数提取高阶统计量（偏度、峰度）和结构特征构建哈希，不依赖额外神经网络训练，并引入混沌映射放大参数微小变化以便定位篡改区域。

Result: 实验表明该方法在盗版检测和篡改定位方面具有有效性和实用价值——哈希具有鲁棒性与判别性，且混沌映射能放大微小参数改动以实现精确定位。

Abstract: With the widespread adoption of deep neural networks (DNNs), protecting
intellectual property and detecting unauthorized tampering of models have
become pressing challenges. Recently, Perceptual hashing has emerged as an
effective approach for identifying pirated models. However, existing methods
either rely on neural networks for feature extraction, demanding substantial
training resources, or suffer from limited applicability and cannot be
universally applied to all convolutional neural networks (CNNs). To address
these limitations, we propose a lightweight CNN model hashing technique that
integrates higher-order statistics (HOS) features with a chaotic mapping
mechanism. Without requiring any auxiliary neural network training, our method
enables efficient piracy detection and precise tampering localization.
Specifically, we extract skewness, kurtosis, and structural features from the
parameters of each network layer to construct a model hash that is both robust
and discriminative. Additionally, we introduce chaotic mapping to amplify minor
changes in model parameters by exploiting the sensitivity of chaotic systems to
initial conditions, thereby facilitating accurate localization of tampered
regions. Experimental results validate the effectiveness and practical value of
the proposed method for model copyright protection and integrity verification.

### [77] [Measuring the Security of Mobile LLM Agents under Adversarial Prompts from Untrusted Third-Party Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27140)
*Chenghao Du,Quanfeng Huang,Tingxuan Tang,Zihao Wang,Yue Xiao*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 首篇系统性研究表明移动LLM代理在现实对抗环境中易被利用，暴露低门槛与复杂攻击路径，呼吁增强防护与模型/系统层面的缓解措施。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LLM代理在移动应用中日益普及，其在对抗性移动环境下的安全性尚未被系统研究，因此作者旨在填补该空白，评估实用场景中的安全威胁。

Method: 作者设计并评估了一系列对抗性用例，包括从弹窗广告到端到端恶意工作流，覆盖8个主流移动代理、3种架构，进行2000+次对抗及对照试验，并将攻击映射到MITRE ATT&CK Mobile框架。

Result: 实验显示：欺诈广告成功率超过80%；高级多应用代理能稳定完成绕过系统警告的恶意流程；揭示了LLM自动化带来的新型特权提升与持久化途径。

Conclusion: 本文得出移动端基于大语言模型（LLM）的代理存在系统性安全风险，低成本攻击（如欺诈广告）和复杂多应用工作流（如恶意软件安装与跨应用数据外泄）均能成功。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have transformed software development, enabling
AI-powered applications known as LLM-based agents that promise to automate

deploying such agents in adversarial mobile environments remain poorly
understood. In this paper, we present the first systematic study of security
risks in mobile LLM agents. We design and evaluate a suite of adversarial case
studies, ranging from opportunistic manipulations such as pop-up advertisements
to advanced, end-to-end workflows involving malware installation and cross-app
data exfiltration. Our evaluation covers eight state-of-the-art mobile agents
across three architectures, with over 2,000 adversarial and paired benign
trials. The results reveal systemic vulnerabilities: low-barrier vectors such
as fraudulent ads succeed with over 80% reliability, while even workflows
requiring the circumvention of operating-system warnings, such as malware
installation, are consistently completed by advanced multi-app agents. By
mapping these attacks to the MITRE ATT&CK Mobile framework, we uncover novel
privilege-escalation and persistence pathways unique to LLM-driven automation.
Collectively, our findings provide the first end-to-end evidence that mobile
LLM agents are exploitable in realistic adversarial settings, where untrusted
third-party channels (e.g., ads, embedded webviews, cross-app notifications)
are an inherent part of the mobile ecosystem.

### [78] [Unvalidated Trust: Cross-Stage Vulnerabilities in Large Language Model Architectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27190)
*Dominik Schwarz*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文总结了商业LLM中41种跨阶段风险模式，主张采用零信任架构（溯源强制、上下文封装、计划再验证）并提出Countermind蓝图来缓解这些风险，认为字符串过滤不够。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM被越来越多地集成到自动化多阶段流水线中，阶段间未经验证的信任带来的风险模式成为实际问题，需要系统性识别和防护这些跨阶段漏洞。

Method: 采用机制中心的分类法，对商业LLM中出现的反复风险模式进行归纳和分析；通过案例和模式分析展示输入非中性解释与实现相关响应的普遍性，论证字符串过滤的局限性，并基于零信任思想提出防御原则与Countermind蓝图。

Result: 归纳出41种常见风险模式，证明输入非中性解释会导致实现相关响应和意外状态变更；指出字符串过滤不足以解决问题，提出零信任原则与Countermind蓝图作为防御方案。

Conclusion: 本论文结论是：商业LLM系统中存在41种反复出现的风险模式，这些模式源自处理阶段之间未经验证的信任，导致输入被非中性解释、触发实现相关的响应或在没有明确指令的情况下产生意外的状态变化。针对字符串级别过滤的方案不足以防护这些体系结构失效模式，应采用零信任架构原则，并通过溯源强制、上下文封装和计划再验证来缓解跨阶段漏洞。提出了名为“Countermind”的概念性蓝图用于实现这些防御措施。

Abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly integrated into automated,
multi-stage pipelines, risk patterns that arise from unvalidated trust between
processing stages become a practical concern. This paper presents a
mechanism-centered taxonomy of 41 recurring risk patterns in commercial LLMs.
The analysis shows that inputs are often interpreted non-neutrally and can
trigger implementation-shaped responses or unintended state changes even
without explicit commands. We argue that these behaviors constitute
architectural failure modes and that string-level filtering alone is
insufficient. To mitigate such cross-stage vulnerabilities, we recommend
zero-trust architectural principles, including provenance enforcement, context
sealing, and plan revalidation, and we introduce "Countermind" as a conceptual
blueprint for implementing these defenses.

### [79] [Prevalence of Security and Privacy Risk-Inducing Usage of AI-based Conversational Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27275)
*Kathrin Grosse,Nico Ebert*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 对3270名英国成年人调查显示：CA常规用户中存在显著不安全行为与知识缺口，需改进厂商防护、透明度与对用户的安全指南。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型和对话式代理的广泛使用，用户可能无意中引入安全与隐私风险，但关于此类行为实际发生频率与模式的证据不足，需要调查来补充威胁模型与指导缓解措施。

Method: 在2024年通过Prolific对3270名英国成年人进行问卷调查，识别出每周至少使用一次CA的“常规用户”，并分析其行为（如共享敏感数据、尝试越狱、上传文件）与相关认知（如对数据被用于训练的理解）。

Result: 在常规用户中，多达三分之一表现出可能助长攻击的行为，四分之一曾尝试越狱，半数表示会对数据进行清理（sanitize），大多数不分享敏感信息但极少分享如密码等高度敏感数据。大多数用户不知道其数据会被用于训练且可选择退出。

Conclusion: 研究表明学术上的威胁模型在现实中存在，部分用户行为可能使对话式代理（CA）容易受到攻击，且大多数用户对其数据被用于训练模型及可选择退出机制不了解。

Abstract: Recent improvement gains in large language models (LLMs) have lead to

are vulnerable to an array of threats, including jailbreaks and, for example,
causing remote code execution when fed specific inputs. As a result, users may
unintentionally introduce risks, for example, by uploading malicious files or
disclosing sensitive information. However, the extent to which such user
behaviors occur and thus potentially facilitate exploits remains largely
unclear. To shed light on this issue, we surveyed a representative sample of
3,270 UK adults in 2024 using Prolific. A third of these use CA services such
as ChatGPT or Gemini at least once a week. Of these ``regular users'', up to a
third exhibited behaviors that may enable attacks, and a fourth have tried
jailbreaking (often out of understandable reasons such as curiosity, fun or
information seeking). Half state that they sanitize data and most participants
report not sharing sensitive data. However, few share very sensitive data such
as passwords. The majority are unaware that their data can be used to train
models and that they can opt-out. Our findings suggest that current academic
threat models manifest in the wild, and mitigations or guidelines for the
secure usage of CAs should be developed. In areas critical to security and
privacy, CAs must be equipped with effective AI guardrails to prevent, for
example, revealing sensitive information to curious employees. Vendors need to
increase efforts to prevent the entry of sensitive data, and to create
transparency with regard to data usage policies and settings.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管组织显著增加网络安全预算，但人的因素仍是主要漏洞，研究旨在评估长期持续培训与情绪线索对员工钓鱼易感性的影响。

Method: 在20家机构、1300多名员工中进行为期12个月的纵向实验，发送超13,000封模拟钓鱼邮件，邮件设计包含情绪诱导、个性化和不同感知来源等变量；使用非参数相关与回归模型分析行为响应。

Result: 持续仿真与有针对性的培训在六个月内将被攻破率降低约50%；员工流动导致意识波动；研究公开了邮件模板和源码用于开放科学。

Conclusion: 持续性的网络安全培训和仿钓鱼演练显著降低了员工的钓鱼易感性，六个月内成功被攻破率减半；员工流动对认知水平有负面影响，需要持续培训来维持防护效果。

Abstract: Phishing constitutes more than 90\% of successful cyberattacks globally,
remaining one of the most persistent threats to organizational security.
Despite organizations tripling their cybersecurity budgets between 2015 and
2025, the human factor continues to pose a critical vulnerability. This study
presents a 12-month longitudinal investigation examining how continuous
cybersecurity training and emotional cues affect employee susceptibility to
phishing. The experiment involved 20 organizations and over 1,300 employees who
collectively received more than 13,000 simulated phishing emails engineered
with diverse emotional, contextual, and structural characteristics. Behavioral
responses were analyzed using non-parametric correlation and regression models
to assess the influence of psychological manipulation, message personalization,
and perceived email source. Results demonstrate that sustained phishing
simulations and targeted training programs lead to a significant reduction in
employee susceptibility, halving successful compromise rates within six months.
Additionally, employee turnover introduces measurable fluctuations in awareness
levels, underscoring the necessity of maintaining continuous training
initiatives. These findings provide one of the few long-term perspectives on
phishing awareness efficacy, highlighting the strategic importance of ongoing
behavioral interventions in strengthening organizational cyber resilience. In
order to support open science, we published our email templates, source code,
and other materials at https://github.com/CorporatePhishingStudy

Abstract: With the rise of location-based service (LBS) applications that rely on

*David Shi,Kevin Joo*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: TraceRank用支付交易作为背书，按金额和时间衰减传播预先赋值的地址信誉，并与语义搜索结合，从而在x402生态中优先展示由高信誉用户支持的服务，并能抵抗Sybil攻击。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着代理对x402上HTTP服务的频繁调用，发现（发现可信且高质量的服务）成为关键问题；需要一种能抵御Sybil攻击并避免仅依赖交易量或基础设施偏见的排名方法。

Method: 对地址进行预计算信誉赋值（可能基于历史行为或链上特征），然后沿支付图按交易金额和时间衰减传播信誉；将传播后得分与语义搜索结合，用于响应自然语言查询。

Result: 在对x402支付图的应用中，TraceRank能把高信誉用户偏好的服务排在前面，而不是仅按交易量排序；理论上对抗Sybil攻击有优势；与语义搜索结合能提升自然语言查询的结果质量。

Conclusion: TraceRank通过将支付交易视为背书并在支付流中传播预计算好信誉度的地址权重，从而在x402生态中实现了基于信誉的服务排名，优先展示由高信誉用户支持的服务。

Abstract: x402 enables Hypertext Transfer Protocol (HTTP) services like application
programming interfaces (APIs), data feeds, and inference providers to accept
cryptocurrency payments for access. As agents increasingly consume these
services, discovery becomes critical: which swap interface should an agent
trust? Which data provider is the most reliable? We introduce TraceRank, a
reputation-weighted ranking algorithm where payment transactions serve as
endorsements. TraceRank seeds addresses with precomputed reputation metrics and
propagates reputation through payment flows weighted by transaction value and
temporal recency. Applied to x402's payment graph, this surfaces services
preferred by high-reputation users rather than those with high transaction
volume. Our system combines TraceRank with semantic search to respond to
natural language queries with high quality results. We argue that reputation
propagation resists Sybil attacks by making spam services with many
low-reputation payers rank below legitimate services with few high-reputation
payers. Ultimately, we aim to construct a search method for x402 enabled
services that avoids infrastructure bias and has better performance than purely
volume based or semantic methods.

### [84] [Best Practices for Biorisk Evaluations on Open-Weight Bio-Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27629)
*Boyi Wei,Zora Che,Nathaniel Li,Udari Madhushani Sehwag,Jasper Götting,Samira Nedungadi,Julian Michael,Summer Yue,Dan Hendrycks,Peter Henderson,Zifan Wang,Seth Donoughe,Mantas Mazeika*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 仅靠预训练数据过滤难以彻底消除模型的双重用途风险，需发展更健壮的安全策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放权重的生物基础模型可能被滥用用于开发生物武器，当前以过滤预训练数据为主的应对措施其有效性尚不明确，需建立评估方法验证其鲁棒性。

Method: 提出Eval框架，从序列建模、突变效应预测和致病性预测三方面评估模型对病毒相关知识的掌握；使用精调与线性探测等方法测试过滤效果与预训练表示中的双重用途信号。

Result: 实验证明被排除的知识在某些情况下可通过精调迅速恢复，并在序列建模中展现更广泛的泛化能力；预训练表示中已存在可通过线性探针唤起的双重用途信号。

Abstract: Open-weight bio-foundation models present a dual-use dilemma. While holding
great promise for accelerating scientific research and drug development, they
could also enable bad actors to develop more deadly bioweapons. To mitigate the
risk posed by these models, current approaches focus on filtering biohazardous
data during pre-training. However, the effectiveness of such an approach
remains unclear, particularly against determined actors who might fine-tune
these models for malicious use. To address this gap, we propose \eval, a
framework to evaluate the robustness of procedures that are intended to reduce
the dual-use capabilities of bio-foundation models. \eval assesses models'
virus understanding through three lenses, including sequence modeling,
mutational effects prediction, and virulence prediction. Our results show that
current filtering practices may not be particularly effective: Excluded
knowledge can be rapidly recovered in some cases via fine-tuning, and exhibits
broader generalizability in sequence modeling. Furthermore, dual-use signals
may already reside in the pretrained representations, and can be elicited via
simple linear probing. These findings highlight the challenges of data
filtering as a standalone procedure, underscoring the need for further research
into robust safety and security strategies for open-weight bio-foundation
models.

### [85] [FlowMesh: A Service Fabric for Composable LLM Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26913)
*Junyi Shen,Noppanat Wadlom,Lingfeng Zhou,Dequan Wang,Xu Miao,Lei Fang,Yao Lu*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: FlowMesh 将 AI 管道拆成可复用的算子并通过全局控制平面统一批次与调度，在异构 GPU 环境下实现显著降本降能并保持低延迟与高弹性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代 AI 部署趋向于由数据变换、微调与智能体交互组成的管道化工作负载，传统孤立的 LLM 作业调度不能有效复用及优化跨用户/跨任务的重复计算与资源分配。

Method: 将工作流分解为带有血统记录的细粒度算子；全局控制平面维护就绪算子池，并用单一效用函数在批次与工作节点间做权衡；数据平面由无状态工作节点和内容寻址存储支撑以实现弹性扩展与可移植性。

Result: 相较基线，FlowMesh 在成本上最多降低 3.8 倍、能耗降低 2.0 倍，延迟表现相当或更优，并在动态及易出错环境下保持高效。

Conclusion: FlowMesh 提出了一种将多用户 AI 工作负载作为共享服务执行和优化的架构，能够跨用户重复消除、按硬件批处理并保留工作流来源，实现更高效的资源利用和更低成本/能耗。

Abstract: AI deployment increasingly resembles a pipeline of data transformation,
fine-tuning, and agent interactions rather than a monolithic LLM job; recent
examples include RLHF/RLAIF training and agentic workflows. To cope with this
shift, we propose FlowMesh, a multi-tenant service fabric that executes and
optimizes these workloads as one shared service instead of isolated pipelines.
It decomposes workflows into fine-grained operators with recorded lineage,
enabling de-duplication of work across users and batching requests on the same
hardware while preserving per-workflow provenance. A global control plane
maintains a cluster-wide pool of ready operators and uses a single utility
function to pick both the batch and the worker, balancing throughput, cost, and
data locality on heterogeneous GPUs. The data plane is an elastic fleet of
stateless workers backed by a content-addressable store, enabling rapid,
automatic scale-out, safe retry after preemption, and portability across
managed clusters such as Kubernetes and geo-distributed GPU marketplaces such
as Vast.ai. Compared with baseline solutions, FlowMesh achieves up to 3.8x cost
reduction and 2.0x lower energy usage, provides a similar or better latency
profile, and remains efficient under dynamic and failure-prone conditions.

</details>

### [87] [Synergistic Tensor and Pipeline Parallelism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27257)
*Mengshi Qi,Jiaxuan Peng,Jie Zhang,Juan Zhu,Yong Li,Huadong Ma*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出一种细粒度编织式TP+PP调度，通过解耦前后向微单元并交织执行，几乎消除TP通信阻塞并降低PP气泡，提升LLM/MLLM训练吞吐量（+12%/+16%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有混合并行方案中，TP带来大量集体通信开销，而PP存在同步不高效（流水线气泡），且现有工作往往只针对其中一项进行优化，未能联合考虑两者的相互影响。

Method: 将PP中的前向与后向传播拆分为细粒度计算单元（micro-ops），并以编织（braid）方式组成复合计算序列，使得不同TP阶段的通信与计算可以更紧密地交错，从而消除TP相关的等待。基于此复合结构，设计PP调度策略以最小化PP气泡。论文通过实现并在LLM与MLLM上评测，比较了与现有调度方法的吞吐量差异。

Result: 实验表明，在相同硬件与模型设置下，提出的方法相较于现有调度方法，LLM训练吞吐量提升最高约12%，MLLM提升最高约16%；并已开源实现。

Conclusion: 本论文提出了一种将张量并行(TP)与流水线并行(PP)协同调度的新方法，通过将正向和反向传播细化为更小的计算单元并交织执行，几乎消除了TP导致的通信阻塞，同时通过定制的PP调度进一步减小流水线气泡，从而提升了分布式训练吞吐量。

Abstract: In the machine learning system, the hybrid model parallelism combining tensor
parallelism (TP) and pipeline parallelism (PP) has become the dominant solution
for distributed training of Large Language Models~(LLMs) and Multimodal LLMs
(MLLMs). However, TP introduces significant collective communication overheads,
while PP suffers from synchronization inefficiencies such as pipeline bubbles.
Existing works primarily address these challenges from isolated perspectives,
focusing either on overlapping TP communication or on flexible PP scheduling to
mitigate pipeline bubbles. In this paper, we propose a new synergistic tensor
and pipeline parallelism schedule that simultaneously reduces both types of
bubbles. Our proposed schedule decouples the forward and backward passes in PP
into fine-grained computation units, which are then braided to form a composite
computation sequence. This compositional structure enables near-complete
elimination of TP-related bubbles. Building upon this structure, we further
design the PP schedule to minimize PP bubbles. Experimental results demonstrate
that our approach improves training throughput by up to 12% for LLMs and 16%
for MLLMs compared to existing scheduling methods. Our source code is avaiable
at https://github.com/MICLAB-BUPT/STP.

</details>


### [88] [A Digital Twin-based Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning Framework for Vehicle-to-Grid Coordination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27289)
*Zhengchang Hua,Panagiotis Oikonomou,Karim Djemame,Nikos Tziritas,Georgios Theodoropoulos*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出DT-MADDPG：通过协作数字孪生构建预测全局模型，增强MADDPG的中心化critic，在不收集敏感原始数据情况下实现接近MADDPG的协调性能，兼顾隐私与去中心化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决在大规模分散控制系统中，如何在不暴露个体隐私的情况下获得全局最优控制策略的问题。传统多智能体学习需集中敏感原始数据，这在现实应用中不切实际，因此需要一种既保持数据隐私又能提供全局信息的学习方案。

Method: 提出一种混合架构：将多智能体深度确定性策略梯度（MADDPG）与协作数字孪生网络结合。关键在于用各个DT共享的隐私保护信息协同构建一个预测全局模型，并将该模型用于增强中心化critic，从而避免收集敏感原始数据。通过仿真辅助学习流程，在V2G仿真环境中训练并评估性能。

Result: 在V2G仿真测试中，DT-MADDPG实现了与标准MADDPG相当的协调效果，同时减少了对敏感原始数据的集中收集，增强了系统的去中心化特点。论文强调了该方法在隐私保护和现实部署可行性方面的优越性。

Conclusion: 本文提出DT-MADDPG算法，通过在中心化critic中引入由各数字孪生协同构建的预测全局模型，实现了在保证隐私的前提下对大规模分散系统（如V2G网络中电动车队）的有效协调。实验表明在仿真环境下，DT-MADDPG在协调性能上可与传统MADDPG相媲美，同时显著提升数据隐私保护和架构去中心化程度，具有实用性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: The coordination of large-scale, decentralised systems, such as a fleet of
Electric Vehicles (EVs) in a Vehicle-to-Grid (V2G) network, presents a
significant challenge for modern control systems. While collaborative Digital
Twins have been proposed as a solution to manage such systems without
compromising the privacy of individual agents, deriving globally optimal
control policies from the high-level information they share remains an open
problem. This paper introduces Digital Twin Assisted Multi-Agent Deep
Deterministic Policy Gradient (DT-MADDPG) algorithm, a novel hybrid
architecture that integrates a multi-agent reinforcement learning framework
with a collaborative DT network. Our core contribution is a simulation-assisted
learning algorithm where the centralised critic is enhanced by a predictive
global model that is collaboratively built from the privacy-preserving data
shared by individual DTs. This approach removes the need for collecting
sensitive raw data at a centralised entity, a requirement of traditional
multi-agent learning algorithms. Experimental results in a simulated V2G
environment demonstrate that DT-MADDPG can achieve coordination performance
comparable to the standard MADDPG algorithm while offering significant
advantages in terms of data privacy and architectural decentralisation. This
work presents a practical and robust framework for deploying intelligent,
learning-based coordination in complex, real-world cyber-physical systems.

</details>

### [90] [ML-Based Optimum Sub-system Size Heuristic for the GPU Implementation of the Tridiagonal Partition Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27351)
*Milena Veneva*

Main category: cs.DC

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CUDA实现的并行划分算法性能依赖于子系统的规模，因而需要一种自动化、经验驱动的方法来预测并选择最优子系统规模以提升性能。

Method: 通过对不同规模SLAE进行计算实验，经验性寻找最优子系统大小；使用kNN分类器对最优子系统大小建模；对结果进行统计分析，并将启发式方法扩展到递归并行划分算法，构造确定每个递归步最优子系统大小的算法；基于kNN预测递归步数。

Conclusion: 本文提出了基于机器学习的启发式方法，用于为并行划分算法的CUDA实现确定最优子系统规模，方法合理且在实验中表现可接受。

Abstract: This paper presents a machine learning (ML)-based heuristic for finding the
optimum sub-system size for the CUDA implementation of the parallel partition
algorithm. Computational experiments for different system of linear algebraic
equation (SLAE) sizes are conducted, and the optimum sub-system size for each
of them is found empirically. To estimate a model for the sub-system size, we
perform the k-nearest neighbors (kNN) classification method. Statistical
analysis of the results is done. By comparing the predicted values with the
actual data, the algorithm is deemed to be acceptably good. Next, the heuristic
is expanded to work for the recursive parallel partition algorithm as well. An
algorithm for determining the optimum sub-system size for each recursive step
is formulated. A kNN model for predicting the optimum number of recursive steps
for a particular SLAE size is built.

### [91] [RDMA Point-to-Point Communication for LLM Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27656)
*Nandor Licker,Kevin Hu,Vladimir Zaytsev,Lequn Chen*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: TransferEngine 是一个跨 NIC 的点对点传输抽象，利用 WriteImm + ImmCounter 实现高吞吐与低延迟，支持多 NIC 聚合，具有很好的可移植性并在多种 LLM 场景中显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代 LLM 系统出现了需要灵活点对点通信的新模式（如分离推理、MoE 路由和异步强化学习微调），现有实现被绑定到特定 NIC，限制了推理引擎集成与硬件可移植性，因此需要一个可移植的通用传输层。

Method: 通过抽象常见 NIC 功能，暴露一侧写入（WriteImm）与 ImmCounter 原语，并实现多 NIC 聚合、无序传输管理与高效完成通知。实现上同时支持 NVIDIA ConnectX-7 与 AWS EFA，优化吞吐和延迟。

Result: 在 ConnectX-7 和 EFA 上均达到 400 Gbps 峰值吞吐。在三个生产系统中验证：KvCache 分离推理与动态伸缩；RL 权重更新对万亿参数模型的 1.3 秒更新延迟；MoE dispatch/combine 在 ConnectX-7 上超越 DeepEP 的解码延迟，并首次在 EFA 上实现可行延迟。

Conclusion: TransferEngine 提供了一个与 NIC 无关的统一点对点传输接口，支持一侧写入带即时（WriteImm）操作和基于 ImmCounter 的完成通知，从而消除了网络顺序假设并透明管理每 GPU 多 NIC 环境。

Abstract: Emerging Large Language Model (LLM) system patterns, such as disaggregated
inference, Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) routing, and asynchronous reinforcement
fine-tuning, require flexible point-to-point communication beyond simple
collectives. Existing implementations are locked to specific Network Interface
Controllers (NICs), hindering integration into inference engines and
portability across hardware providers. We present TransferEngine, which bridges
the functionality of common NICs to expose a uniform interface. TransferEngine
exposes one-sided WriteImm operations with a ImmCounter primitive for
completion notification, without ordering assumptions of network transport,
transparently managing multiple NICs per GPU. We demonstrate peak throughput of
400 Gbps on both NVIDIA ConnectX-7 and AWS Elastic Fabric Adapter (EFA). We
showcase TransferEngine through three production systems: (1) KvCache transfer
for disaggregated inference with dynamic scaling, (2) RL weight updates
achieving 1.3 seconds for trillion-parameter models, and (3) MoE
dispatch/combine implementation exceeding DeepEP decode latency on ConnectX-7,
with the first viable latencies on EFA. We demonstrate that our portable
point-to-point communication complements collectives while avoiding lock-in.

</details>

### [92] [Trace-driven Path Emulation of Satellite Networks using Hypatia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27027)
*Martin Ottens,Kai-Steffen Hielscher,Reinhard German*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 通过在Hypatia中记录网络路径特性并在实时环境重放Trace，本文实现了仿真与真实系统的联动评估，对LEO卫星网络下协议和应用行为的评估准确性高，相关性最高达0.96，但仍存在反馈与同步方面的挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LEO卫星巨型星座快速增加，需评估现有互联网协议和应用在此新环境下的表现；传统离散事件模拟器无法直接在真实应用与用户交互场景中验证协议行为，需桥接仿真与实时测试平台。

Method: 在扩展Hypatia框架中，进行非实时仿真并在仿真过程中记录端到端路径特性，导出为Trace文件；在实时仿真/仿真环境中重放这些Trace，以对真实软件和用户交互场景进行评估。实验对不同卫星星座和场景进行对比，使用完整仿真作为基线，并通过统计相关性指标（最高达0.96）评估重放的准确性。

Result: 在多种星座和场景下，Trace重放在实时环境中能较精准再现仿真中的路径特性，与完整仿真结果具有高相关性（最高0.96）。文中也讨论了局限与挑战，如缺乏仿真到仿真-实时的反馈通路及同步问题。

Conclusion: 论文提出一种基于Trace驱动的LEO卫星网络仿真与真实系统联动的方案，通过在Hypatia离散事件模拟器中记录网络路径特性（时延、带宽等），生成Trace文件并在实时仿真环境中重放，从而在真实主机上评估应用和协议行为。结果显示仿真与真实重放之间具备高相关性，验证了方法的有效性。

Abstract: The increasing prevalence LEO satellite mega-constellations for global
Internet coverage requires new approaches to evaluate the behavior of existing
Internet protocols and applications. Traditional discrete event simulators like
Hypatia allow for modeling these environments but fall short in evaluating real
applications. This paper builds upon our previous work, in which we proposed a
system design for trace-driven emulation of such satellite networks, bridging
the gab between simulations and real-time testbeds. By extending the Hypatia
framework, we record network path characteristics, e.g., delay and bandwidth,
between two endpoints in the network during non-real-time simulations. Path
characteristics are exported to Trace Files, which are replayed in real-time
emulation environments on real systems, enabling evaluations with real software
and human interaction. An advantage of our approach is its easy adaptability to
existing simulation models. Our extensive evaluation involves multiple
scenarios with different satellite constellations, illustrating the approach's
accuracy in reproducing the behavior of satellite networks. Between full
simulation, which serves as a baseline for our evaluation, and emulation runs,
we observe high correlation metrics of up to 0.96, validating the approach's
effectiveness. Challenges such as the lack of emulation-to-simulation feedback
and synchronization issues are discussed.

</details>


### [93] [TheaterQ: A Qdisc for Dynamic Network Emulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27057)
*Martin Ottens,Kai-Steffen Hielscher,Reinhard German*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: TheaterQ is a kernel qdisc for dynamic, microsecond-resolution trace-driven network emulation, accurate and efficient, supporting synchronization and multiple impairment types; open-source under GPLv2.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Static-parameter emulators (e.g., NetEm) cannot capture rapid, dynamic changes in real networks needed for modern protocol development; a kernel-level, trace-driven emulator with fine time resolution is required.

Method: Implements a Linux kernel qdisc that reads Trace Files specifying timelines of network characteristics, updates emulation states at up to 1 microsecond resolution without userspace involvement, synchronizes multiple qdiscs, and handles delay shaping, bandwidth control, loss, duplication, and reordering.

Result: Evaluation demonstrates high emulation accuracy and comparable performance to existing tools, validating TheaterQ as a flexible, efficient solution for dynamic network emulation.

Conclusion: TheaterQ introduces a high-precision, kernel-level qdisc for dynamic network emulation, overcoming static limitations of tools like NetEm and enabling microsecond-resolution updates via Trace Files; it synchronizes across instances and supports delay, bandwidth, loss, duplication, and reordering with accuracy and performance comparable to existing tools, released under GPLv2.

Abstract: TheaterQ is a Linux qdisc designed for dynamic network emulation, addressing
the limitations of static parameters in traditional tools like NetEm. By
utilizing Trace Files containing timelines with network characteristics,
TheaterQ achieves high-accuracy emulation of dynamic networks without involving
the userspace and allows for resolutions of characteristic updates of up to 1
microsecond. Features include synchronization across mutliple qdisc instances
and handling of delays, bandwidth, packet loss, duplication, and reordering.
Evaluations show TheaterQ's accuracy and its comparable performance to existing
tools, offering a flexible solution for modern communication protocol
development. TheaterQ is available as open-source software under the GPLv2
license.

</details>

*Shuo Zhu,Siyu Lin*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 构建基于DTMC的消息生成器和NR-V2X Mode 2分析模型，验证了重评估机制能提高可靠性，但延迟仍需优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: V2X无线环境复杂（大量消息、不规则报文、高速移动），导致资源冲突效率低，需在MAC层提升性能，3GPP在NR-V2X引入重评估机制以持续感知资源避免冲突，研究该机制效果。

Method: 建立NR-V2X Mode 2的分析模型，并用离散时间马尔可夫链（DTMC）构建符合3GPP推荐的高级V2X业务流量模式的消息生成器。

Abstract: Massive message transmissions, unpredictable aperiodic messages, and
high-speed moving vehicles contribute to the complex wireless environment,
resulting in inefficient resource collisions in Vehicle to Everything (V2X). In
order to achieve better medium access control (MAC) layer performance, 3GPP
introduced several new features in NR-V2X. One of the most important is the
re-evaluation mechanism. It allows the vehicle to continuously sense resources
before message transmission to avoid resource collisions. So far, only a few
articles have studied the re-evaluation mechanism of NR-V2X, and they mainly
focus on network simulator that do not consider variable traffic, which makes
analysis and comparison difficult. In this paper, an analytical model of NR-V2X
Mode 2 is established, and a message generator is constructed by using discrete
time Markov chain (DTMC) to simulate the traffic pattern recommended by 3GPP
advanced V2X services. Our study shows that the re-evaluation mechanism
improves the reliability of NR-V2X transmission, but there are still local
improvements needed to reduce latency.

### [95] [Stochastic Geometry of Cylinders: Characterizing Inter-Nodal Distances for 3D UAV Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27111)
*Yunfeng Jiang,Zhiming Huang,Jianping Pan*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文首次给出在圆柱体内由二项点过程建模的有限三维无线网络覆盖概率的精确解析框架，方法基于独立性、卷积几何与拉普拉斯变换导数，理论与仿真匹配良好，可推广至多种受限3D场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限节点、三维且有界的无线网络中，传统的泊松点过程近似失效，导致覆盖概率分析缺乏精确解析表达，且三维有界几何带来距离-干扰耦合问题，亟需一个精确且可计算的分析工具。

Method: 利用独立性结构、卷积几何和拉普拉斯变换的导数性质构建分析——通过分解干扰和信号距分布，采用卷积积分和拉普拉斯域求导获得可计算的闭式或半闭式表达，从而实现数学精确且计算高效的公式。

Result: 推导出适用于圆柱体约束的有限三维网络的覆盖概率表达式；仿真结果与蒙特卡罗模拟高度一致，并显著优于基于泊松过程的近似；方法可推广到空中、水下和机器人等任意受限3D无线系统。

Conclusion: 本论文给出了一个用于有限三维无线网络（在圆柱区域内由二项点过程建模）的精确覆盖概率分析框架，解决了有限节点设置下空间相关性和有界几何中链路距离与干扰耦合带来的难题。

Abstract: The analytical characterization of coverage probability in finite
three-dimensional wireless networks has long remained an open problem, hindered
by the loss of spatial independence in finite-node settings and the coupling
between link distances and interference in bounded geometries. This paper
closes this gap by presenting the first exact analytical framework for coverage
probability in finite 3D networks modeled by a binomial point process within a
cylindrical region. To bypass the intractability that has long hindered such
analyses, we leverage the independence structure, convolution geometry, and
derivative properties of Laplace transforms, yielding a formulation that is
both mathematically exact and computationally efficient. Extensive Monte Carlo
simulations verify the analysis and demonstrate significant accuracy gains over
conventional Poisson-based models. The results generalize to any confined 3D
wireless system, including aerial, underwater, and robotic networks.

</details>

Method: 利用XGBoost进行节点移动性预测，并结合信号强度与空间接近度的复合优化策略来选择簇头；在集中式（5G）与去中心化（6G）拓扑下使用真实视频流量进行仿真验证。

Result: 在去中心化（6G）场景下，所提方法显著降低时延和抖动并提高吞吐量，展示了在可扩展性与稳定性方面的优势。

{Extreme Gradient Boosting (XGBoost)} and a composite optimization strategy
based on signal strength and spatial proximity to identify optimal cluster
heads. To evaluate the proposed method, comprehensive simulations were
conducted in both centralized (5G) and decentralized (6G) topologies using
realistic video traffic patterns. Results show that the proposed model achieves
significant improvements in delay, jitter, and throughput in decentralized
scenarios. These findings demonstrate the potential of combining machine
learning with clustering techniques to enhance scalability, stability, and
performance in next-generation aerial networks.
